  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {
    background: none;
  }
  a, chops-button, a.button, .button, .linkify {
    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;
    font-weight: var(--chops-link-font-weight);
    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {
    filter: brightness(95%);
  }
  chops-button, a.button, .button {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
    background: var(--chops-white);

    margin: 0;
    margin-left: auto;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    padding: var(--chops-button-padding);
  }
  chops-button i.material-icons, a.button i.material-icons, .button i.material-icons {
    display: block;
    margin-right: 4px;
  }
  chops-button.emphasized, a.button.emphasized, .button.emphasized {
    background: var(--chops-primary-button-bg);
    color: var(--chops-primary-button-color);
    text-shadow: 1px 1px 3px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.25);
  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.
  */
  .medium-heading {
    font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);

        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





|source_client_|[1] keep a raw pointer of XDragDropClient[2]. And it could be accessed[3] when handling dispatched events even after the source window has been destroyed.



<span class="line"><!---->|source_client_|[1] keep a raw pointer of XDragDropClient[2]. And it could be accessed[3] when handling dispatched events even after the source window has been destroyed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1]. 



<span class="line"><!---->[1]. <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:ui/base/x/x11_drag_context.h;l=78;drc=0c59d7a7073f14e600491fd2eba187f5684c3224;bpv=0;bpt=0



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:ui/base/x/x11_drag_context.h;l=78;drc=0c59d7a7073f14e600491fd2eba187f5684c3224;bpv=0;bpt=0"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:ui/base/x/x11_drag_context.h;l=78;drc=0c59d7a7073f14e600491fd2eba187f5684c3224;bpv=0;bpt=0<!----></a>



<br>





[2]. 



<span class="line"><!---->[2]. <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:ui/base/x/x11_drag_drop_client.cc;l=309;drc=2a460ccaa47f04efefa45cc127aa57cc51a999b7



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:ui/base/x/x11_drag_drop_client.cc;l=309;drc=2a460ccaa47f04efefa45cc127aa57cc51a999b7"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:ui/base/x/x11_drag_drop_client.cc;l=309;drc=2a460ccaa47f04efefa45cc127aa57cc51a999b7<!----></a>



<br>





[3]. 



<span class="line"><!---->[3]. <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:ui/base/x/x11_drag_context.cc;l=173;drc=d2169dbe1a3c4162e7b25550181ac261e0f26287



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:ui/base/x/x11_drag_context.cc;l=173;drc=d2169dbe1a3c4162e7b25550181ac261e0f26287"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/master:ui/base/x/x11_drag_context.cc;l=173;drc=d2169dbe1a3c4162e7b25550181ac261e0f26287<!----></a>

Security sheriff: I can reproduce this with a linux ASAN release build but not a debug build, although it took me a couple tries. Setting some initial labels: This looks like a UAF in the browser process, but it requires user interaction to trigger so it doesn't seem like it would be exploitable in a drive-by fashion, so setting Severity-High. Reporter: I'd be interested if you can think of a way to reduce or remove the user interaction requirement (with our without a compromised renderer), which might make this a Sev-Critical.



<span class="line"><!---->Security sheriff: I can reproduce this with a linux ASAN release build but not a debug build, although it took me a couple tries. Setting some initial labels: This looks like a UAF in the browser process, but it requires user interaction to trigger so it doesn't seem like it would be exploitable in a drive-by fashion, so setting Severity-High. Reporter: I'd be interested if you can think of a way to reduce or remove the user interaction requirement (with our without a compromised renderer), which might make this a Sev-Critical.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





thomasanderson@ could you PTAL? Also cc'ing adunaev@ who also appears active in x11_drag_drop_client.cc.

@cthomp: 



<span class="line"><!---->@cthomp: <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





With a compromised renderer, the bug can be easily triggered through |StartDragging|-IPC[1] without any user interaction. I uploaded a renderer patch and poc to do this. 



<span class="line"><!---->With a compromised renderer, the bug can be easily triggered through |StartDragging|-IPC[1] without any user interaction. I uploaded a renderer patch and poc to do this. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Without a compromised renderer, I have no idea how to completely remove the user interaction. But I think the drag-and-drop is a very common operation when users browse the web, it can happen to not only images but also other elements such as text and links.



<span class="line"><!---->Without a compromised renderer, I have no idea how to completely remove the user interaction. But I think the drag-and-drop is a very common operation when users browse the web, it can happen to not only images but also other elements such as text and links.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<br>



<br>





[x11] Fixed UAF in drag and drop.



<span class="line"><!---->[x11] Fixed UAF in drag and drop.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To short-cut round trips to the X server when drag and drop happens



<span class="line"><!---->To short-cut round trips to the X server when drag and drop happens<!----></span>



<br>





between two Chromium windows, XDragContext stored the raw pointer to



<span class="line"><!---->between two Chromium windows, XDragContext stored the raw pointer to<!----></span>



<br>





XDragDropClient of the source window in its source_client_ attribute.



<span class="line"><!---->XDragDropClient of the source window in its source_client_ attribute.<!----></span>



<br>





This made possible to access the deleted object (use after free) if the



<span class="line"><!---->This made possible to access the deleted object (use after free) if the<!----></span>



<br>





source window had been destroyed during the operation.  In short,



<span class="line"><!---->source window had been destroyed during the operation.  In short,<!----></span>



<br>





although the target context can call the source client directly via the



<span class="line"><!---->although the target context can call the source client directly via the<!----></span>



<br>





shortcut, the PropertyNotify event comes from the X server (not using



<span class="line"><!---->shortcut, the PropertyNotify event comes from the X server (not using<!----></span>



<br>





the shortcut), and apparently it can come to the target context after



<span class="line"><!---->the shortcut), and apparently it can come to the target context after<!----></span>



<br>





the source window and its client had been destroyed but before the



<span class="line"><!---->the source window and its client had been destroyed but before the<!----></span>



<br>





target context is notified.  See the issue for full details.



<span class="line"><!---->target context is notified.  See the issue for full details.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Here the XDragContext::source_client_ is removed, and all its uses



<span class="line"><!---->Here the XDragContext::source_client_ is removed, and all its uses<!----></span>



<br>





are replaced with getting the client from the global map of clients



<span class="line"><!---->are replaced with getting the client from the global map of clients<!----></span>



<br>





[1]. The client removes itself from the map upon destruction [2] so



<span class="line"><!---->[1]. The client removes itself from the map upon destruction [2] so<!----></span>



<br>





this change eliminates the vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->this change eliminates the vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For the record, there is the test in the interactive_ui_tests suite



<span class="line"><!---->For the record, there is the test in the interactive_ui_tests suite<!----></span>



<br>





(namely BookmarkBarViewTest22.CloseSourceBrowserDuringDrag) that should



<span class="line"><!---->(namely BookmarkBarViewTest22.CloseSourceBrowserDuringDrag) that should<!----></span>



<br>





emulate this situation but is has some flaws [3].



<span class="line"><!---->emulate this situation but is has some flaws [3].<!----></span>



<br>

Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?

- Chrome:

<span class="line"><!---->2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->4. Does this change need to be merged into other active release branches (M-1, M+1)?<!----></span>



<br>





5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?



<span class="line"><!---->5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?<!----></span>

6. Is this a new feature?

<span class="line"><!---->Chrome OS Only:<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. <span class="line"><!---->Date: Mon Dec 14 18:55:03 2020<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[x11] Fixed UAF in drag and drop.



<span class="line"><!---->[x11] Fixed UAF in drag and drop.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To short-cut round trips to the X server when drag and drop happens



<span class="line"><!---->To short-cut round trips to the X server when drag and drop happens<!----></span>



<br>





between two Chromium windows, XDragContext stored the raw pointer to



<span class="line"><!---->between two Chromium windows, XDragContext stored the raw pointer to<!----></span>



<br>





XDragDropClient of the source window in its source_client_ attribute.



<span class="line"><!---->XDragDropClient of the source window in its source_client_ attribute.<!----></span>



<br>





This made possible to access the deleted object (use after free) if the



<span class="line"><!---->This made possible to access the deleted object (use after free) if the<!----></span>



<br>





source window had been destroyed during the operation.  In short,



<span class="line"><!---->source window had been destroyed during the operation.  In short,<!----></span>



<br>





although the target context can call the source client directly via the



<span class="line"><!---->although the target context can call the source client directly via the<!----></span>



<br>





shortcut, the PropertyNotify event comes from the X server (not using



<span class="line"><!---->shortcut, the PropertyNotify event comes from the X server (not using<!----></span>



<br>





the shortcut), and apparently it can come to the target context after



<span class="line"><!---->the shortcut), and apparently it can come to the target context after<!----></span>



<br>





the source window and its client had been destroyed but before the



<span class="line"><!---->the source window and its client had been destroyed but before the<!----></span>



<br>





target context is notified.  See the issue for full details.



<span class="line"><!---->target context is notified.  See the issue for full details.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Here the XDragContext::source_client_ is removed, and all its uses



<span class="line"><!---->Here the XDragContext::source_client_ is removed, and all its uses<!----></span>



<br>





are replaced with getting the client from the global map of clients



<span class="line"><!---->are replaced with getting the client from the global map of clients<!----></span>



<br>





[1]. The client removes itself from the map upon destruction [2] so



<span class="line"><!---->[1]. The client removes itself from the map upon destruction [2] so<!----></span>



<br>





this change eliminates the vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->this change eliminates the vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For the record, there is the test in the interactive_ui_tests suite



<span class="line"><!---->For the record, there is the test in the interactive_ui_tests suite<!----></span>



<br>





(namely BookmarkBarViewTest22.CloseSourceBrowserDuringDrag) that should



<span class="line"><!---->(namely BookmarkBarViewTest22.CloseSourceBrowserDuringDrag) that should<!----></span>



<br>





emulate this situation but is has some flaws [3].



<span class="line"><!---->emulate this situation but is has some flaws [3].<!----></span>



<br>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/36aba5e75bfddda35e8088a9c23e08f8940694f9"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/36aba5e75bfddda35e8088a9c23e08f8940694f9<!----></a>

commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





36aba5e75bfddda35e8088a9c23e08f8940694f9



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/36aba5e75bfddda35e8088a9c23e08f8940694f9"><!---->36aba5e75bfddda35e8088a9c23e08f8940694f9<!----></a>

Author: Alexander Dunaev <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Alexander Dunaev &lt;<!----></span>





adunaev@igalia.com



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/adunaev@igalia.com"><!---->adunaev@igalia.com<!----></a>

<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Wed Dec 16 03:51:31 2020



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Wed Dec 16 03:51:31 2020<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[x11] Fixed UAF in drag and drop.



<span class="line"><!---->[x11] Fixed UAF in drag and drop.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To short-cut round trips to the X server when drag and drop happens



<span class="line"><!---->To short-cut round trips to the X server when drag and drop happens<!----></span>



<br>





between two Chromium windows, XDragContext stored the raw pointer to



<span class="line"><!---->between two Chromium windows, XDragContext stored the raw pointer to<!----></span>



<br>





XDragDropClient of the source window in its source_client_ attribute.



<span class="line"><!---->XDragDropClient of the source window in its source_client_ attribute.<!----></span>



<br>





This made possible to access the deleted object (use after free) if the



<span class="line"><!---->This made possible to access the deleted object (use after free) if the<!----></span>



<br>





source window had been destroyed during the operation.  In short,



<span class="line"><!---->source window had been destroyed during the operation.  In short,<!----></span>



<br>





although the target context can call the source client directly via the



<span class="line"><!---->although the target context can call the source client directly via the<!----></span>



<br>





shortcut, the PropertyNotify event comes from the X server (not using



<span class="line"><!---->shortcut, the PropertyNotify event comes from the X server (not using<!----></span>



<br>





the shortcut), and apparently it can come to the target context after



<span class="line"><!---->the shortcut), and apparently it can come to the target context after<!----></span>



<br>





the source window and its client had been destroyed but before the



<span class="line"><!---->the source window and its client had been destroyed but before the<!----></span>



<br>





target context is notified.  See the issue for full details.



<span class="line"><!---->target context is notified.  See the issue for full details.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Here the XDragContext::source_client_ is removed, and all its uses



<span class="line"><!---->Here the XDragContext::source_client_ is removed, and all its uses<!----></span>



<br>





are replaced with getting the client from the global map of clients



<span class="line"><!---->are replaced with getting the client from the global map of clients<!----></span>



<br>





[1]. The client removes itself from the map upon destruction [2] so



<span class="line"><!---->[1]. The client removes itself from the map upon destruction [2] so<!----></span>



<br>





this change eliminates the vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->this change eliminates the vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For the record, there is the test in the interactive_ui_tests suite



<span class="line"><!---->For the record, there is the test in the interactive_ui_tests suite<!----></span>



<br>





(namely BookmarkBarViewTest22.CloseSourceBrowserDuringDrag) that should



<span class="line"><!---->(namely BookmarkBarViewTest22.CloseSourceBrowserDuringDrag) that should<!----></span>



<br>





emulate this situation but is has some flaws [3].



<span class="line"><!---->emulate this situation but is has some flaws [3].<!----></span>



<br>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/1752fe9fd96012e365e03b8ea97b63c247734603"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/1752fe9fd96012e365e03b8ea97b63c247734603<!----></a>

commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





1752fe9fd96012e365e03b8ea97b63c247734603



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/1752fe9fd96012e365e03b8ea97b63c247734603"><!---->1752fe9fd96012e365e03b8ea97b63c247734603<!----></a>

Author: Alexander Dunaev <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Alexander Dunaev &lt;<!----></span>





adunaev@igalia.com



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/adunaev@igalia.com"><!---->adunaev@igalia.com<!----></a>

<br>





Date: Sat Jan 09 19:56:54 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Sat Jan 09 19:56:54 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[x11] Fixed UAF in drag and drop.



<span class="line"><!---->[x11] Fixed UAF in drag and drop.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





To short-cut round trips to the X server when drag and drop happens



<span class="line"><!---->To short-cut round trips to the X server when drag and drop happens<!----></span>



<br>





between two Chromium windows, XDragContext stored the raw pointer to



<span class="line"><!---->between two Chromium windows, XDragContext stored the raw pointer to<!----></span>



<br>





XDragDropClient of the source window in its source_client_ attribute.



<span class="line"><!---->XDragDropClient of the source window in its source_client_ attribute.<!----></span>



<br>





This made possible to access the deleted object (use after free) if the



<span class="line"><!---->This made possible to access the deleted object (use after free) if the<!----></span>



<br>





source window had been destroyed during the operation.  In short,



<span class="line"><!---->source window had been destroyed during the operation.  In short,<!----></span>



<br>





although the target context can call the source client directly via the



<span class="line"><!---->although the target context can call the source client directly via the<!----></span>



<br>





shortcut, the PropertyNotify event comes from the X server (not using



<span class="line"><!---->shortcut, the PropertyNotify event comes from the X server (not using<!----></span>



<br>





the shortcut), and apparently it can come to the target context after



<span class="line"><!---->the shortcut), and apparently it can come to the target context after<!----></span>



<br>





the source window and its client had been destroyed but before the



<span class="line"><!---->the source window and its client had been destroyed but before the<!----></span>



<br>





target context is notified.  See the issue for full details.



<span class="line"><!---->target context is notified.  See the issue for full details.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Here the XDragContext::source_client_ is removed, and all its uses



<span class="line"><!---->Here the XDragContext::source_client_ is removed, and all its uses<!----></span>



<br>





are replaced with getting the client from the global map of clients



<span class="line"><!---->are replaced with getting the client from the global map of clients<!----></span>



<br>





[1]. The client removes itself from the map upon destruction [2] so



<span class="line"><!---->[1]. The client removes itself from the map upon destruction [2] so<!----></span>



<br>





this change eliminates the vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->this change eliminates the vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For the record, there is the test in the interactive_ui_tests suite



<span class="line"><!---->For the record, there is the test in the interactive_ui_tests suite<!----></span>



<br>





(namely BookmarkBarViewTest22.CloseSourceBrowserDuringDrag) that should



<span class="line"><!---->(namely BookmarkBarViewTest22.CloseSourceBrowserDuringDrag) that should<!----></span>



<br>





emulate this situation but is has some flaws [3].



<span class="line"><!---->emulate this situation but is has some flaws [3].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>
